[[instructions]]
== Instructions
:imagesdir: ../images
:source-highlighter: rouge




AME defines *98* instructions and an additional *2* pseudoinstructions.


Datatype Management::
[cols="1,2",%unbreakable]
!===
| Mnemonic | Name

a| `agettyp xd, ad`
| <<udb:doc:inst:agettyp,Get accumulator datatype>>
a| `asettyp ad, xs1`
| <<udb:doc:inst:asettyp,Set accumulator datatype>>
a| `mgettyp xd, ms1`
| <<udb:doc:inst:mgettyp,Get datatype>>
a| `msettyp md, xs1`
| <<udb:doc:inst:msettyp,Set datatype>>
!===

<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:agettyp]
=== `agettyp`

Synopsis::
Get accumulator datatype

Mnemonic::
`agettyp xd, ad`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xd","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x5,"type":2},{"bits":2,"name": "ad","type":4},{"bits":15,"name": 0x400,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Get the datatype of an `Acc` register by reading from `Ad`.



Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> xd = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<2> ad = $encoding[16:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
X[xd] = Ad[ad];
----


<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:asettyp]
=== `asettyp`

Synopsis::
Set accumulator datatype

Mnemonic::
`asettyp ad, xs1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":8,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":2,"name": "ad","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": 0x14,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x60,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Sets the datatype of an `Acc` register and zeros the data by writing to `Ad` and zeroing `Acc`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
acc = np.zeros_like(acc)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<2> ad = $encoding[9:8];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dtype = X[xs1][31:0];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_datatype_supported,ame_datatype_supported>>pass:[(]dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  Ad[ad] = X[xs1];
  Acc[ad] = 0;
}
----


<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mabs_ew]
=== `mabs.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise absolute value

Mnemonic::
`mabs.ew md, ms1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise absolute value of the tensor in `ms1`, stored into `md`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = np.abs(ms1)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ABS1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, 0)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ABS1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, 0)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src1_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src1_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src1_regno], src1_dtype);
    U32 src1_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src1_element_value = src1_value[src1_hi_idx:src1_lo_idx];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ABS1D, src1_dtype, src1_element_value, src1_dtype, src1_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}
----


<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mabsdiff_ew]
=== `mabsdiff.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise absolute difference

Mnemonic::
`mabsdiff.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x4,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise absolute difference of the tensors in `ms1` and `ms2`, stored into `md`.
Used for L1 distance and error metrics.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = np.abs(ms1 - ms2)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
Bits<32> src2_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ABSDIFF1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src2_nregs == 0) {
    src2_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src2_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src2_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ABSDIFF1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src1_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src1_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src1_regno], src1_dtype);
    U32 src1_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_regno = e / src2_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src2_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src2_regno], src2_dtype);
    U32 src2_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src1_element_value = src1_value[src1_hi_idx:src1_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src2_element_value = src2_value[src2_hi_idx:src2_lo_idx];

  }

[#udb:doc:inst:mabsdiff_ew_x]
=== `mabsdiff.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar absolute difference

Mnemonic::
`mabsdiff.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x5,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Computes the elementwise absolute difference between a scalar constant from integer
register `xs1` and every element of square `ms2`, stored into `md`.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = |xs1 - ms2[i]|`
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = np.abs(xs1 - ms2)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ABSDIFF1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ABSDIFF1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar = X[xs1];
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src_regno = e / src_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src_regno], src_dtype);
    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_element_value = scalar[src_element_size - 1:0];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ABSDIFF1D, src_dtype, scalar_element_value, src_dtype, src_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }

  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {

  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;

    src2_nregs = 1;

    dest_nregs = 1;

    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);

      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);

  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {

    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));

[#udb:doc:inst:mand_ew_x]
=== `mand.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar bitwise AND

Mnemonic::
`mand.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x7,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Computes the elementwise bitwise AND of a scalar constant from integer register `xs1`
with every element of square `ms2`, stored into `md`.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = xs1 & ms2[i]`
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = xs1 & ms2
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::AND1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::AND1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar = X[xs1];
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src_regno = e / src_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src_regno], src_dtype);
    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_element_value = scalar[src_element_size - 1:0];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::AND1D, src_dtype, scalar_element_value, src_dtype, src_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);

=== `mandnot.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise bitwise AND-NOT

Mnemonic::
`mandnot.ew md, ms1, ms2`

+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]

....

Description::

=== `mbcast.x`

Synopsis::
Broadcast integer scalar to all elements of a square

Mnemonic::
`mbcast.x md, xs1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x4,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Broadcasts the scalar value from integer register `xs1` to all element positions of
matrix register `md`.
+
The element size is determined by `Md[md]`. For compute datatypes, all `AME_NELEM`
elements are set to the lower `sizeof(Md[md])` bits of `xs1`. For storage-only datatypes,
all `pack_factor * AME_NELEM` elements are set.
+
If `Md[md]` is uninitialized (zero), `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
np.full_like(md, xs1)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dtype = Md[md];
if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
  if pass:[(]md >= 16) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
}
U32 element_size_bits = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dtype);
if pass:[(]element_size_bits == 0) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 pack_factor = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dtype) ? (AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE / element_size_bits) : 1;
  U32 total_elements = pack_factor * AME_NELEM;
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result = 0;
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar = X[xs1];
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < total_elements; e++) {
    U32 bit_lo = e * element_size_bits;
    U32 bit_hi = bit_lo pass:[+] element_size_bits - 1;
    result[bit_hi:bit_lo] = scalar[element_size_bits - 1:0];
  }
  M[md] = result;
}
----

[#udb:doc:inst:mcmovge_ew]
=== `mcmovge.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise two-way conditional move (non-negative)

Mnemonic::
`mcmovge.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x10,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise two-way conditional move using the non-negative sign of `ms1` as predicate.
+
For each element, `md[i] = ms2[i]` if `ms1[i] >= 0` (sign bit clear),
otherwise `md[i]` is left unchanged.
+
`md` is both a source and destination: when the predicate is false (sign bit set),
the existing element in `md` is preserved.  `ms1` serves as the predicate register:
any non-negative value is treated as true.
+
Complementary to `mcmovlt.1d`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = np.where(ms1 >= 0, ms2, md)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
Bits<32> src2_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MUXGE1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src2_nregs == 0) {
    src2_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src2_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src2_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MUXGE1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src1_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src1_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src1_regno], src1_dtype);
    U32 src1_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_regno = e / src2_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src2_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src2_regno], src2_dtype);
    U32 src2_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> dest_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[md pass:[+] dest_regno], dest_dtype);
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src1_element_value = src1_value[src1_hi_idx:src1_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src2_element_value = src2_value[src2_hi_idx:src2_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> dest_current = dest_value[dest_hi_idx:dest_lo_idx];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MUXGE1D, src1_dtype, src1_element_value, src2_dtype, src2_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}
----

[#udb:doc:inst:mcmovlt_ew]
=== `mcmovlt.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise two-way conditional move (negative)

Mnemonic::
`mcmovlt.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x11,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise two-way conditional move using the sign of `ms1` as predicate.
+
For each element, `md[i] = ms2[i]` if `ms1[i] < 0` (sign bit set),
otherwise `md[i]` is left unchanged.
+
`md` is both a source and destination: when the predicate is false (sign bit clear),
the existing element in `md` is preserved.  `ms1` serves as the predicate register:
any negative value is treated as true.
+
Complementary to `mcmovge.1d`.

[source,python]

[#udb:doc:inst:mcmpge_ew]
=== `mcmpge.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise greater-or-equal compare

Mnemonic::
`mcmpge.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0xc,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise greater-or-equal comparison of the tensors in `ms1` and `ms2`, stored into `md`.
+
For each element, `md[i]` is set to the canonical true value (-1, all bits set) if
`ms1[i] >= ms2[i]`, otherwise `md[i]` is set to the canonical false value (0).
+
Floating-point comparisons follow IEEE 754 semantics.
Complementary to `mcmplt.1d`; both forms are provided to ensure correct behavior
in the presence of NaN, +∞, and −∞.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = (ms1 >= ms2).astype(int) * -1
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
Bits<32> src2_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::CMPGE1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src2_nregs == 0) {
    src2_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src2_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src2_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::CMPGE1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src1_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src1_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src1_regno], src1_dtype);
    U32 src1_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_regno = e / src2_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src2_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src2_regno], src2_dtype);
    U32 src2_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src1_element_value = src1_value[src1_hi_idx:src1_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src2_element_value = src2_value[src2_hi_idx:src2_lo_idx];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::CMPGE1D, src1_dtype, src1_element_value, src2_dtype, src2_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}

[#udb:doc:inst:mcmpge_ew_x]
=== `mcmpge.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar compare greater-or-equal

Mnemonic::
`mcmpge.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0xc,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Compares a scalar constant from integer register `xs1` against every element of square
`ms2`, storing -1 (all bits set) where the scalar is greater than or equal to the element,
and 0 otherwise, into `md`.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = (xs1 >= ms2[i]) ? -1 : 0`
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = (xs1 >= ms2).astype(md.dtype) * -1
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]

} else {

  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::CMPGE1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);

    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);

    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));

[#udb:doc:inst:mcmplt_ew]
=== `mcmplt.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise less-than compare

Mnemonic::
`mcmplt.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0xd,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise less-than comparison of the tensors in `ms1` and `ms2`, stored into `md`.
+
For each element, `md[i]` is set to the canonical true value (-1, all bits set) if
`ms1[i] < ms2[i]`, otherwise `md[i]` is set to the canonical false value (0).
+
Floating-point comparisons follow IEEE 754 semantics.
Complementary to `mcmpge.1d`; both forms are provided to ensure correct behavior
in the presence of NaN, +∞, and −∞.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = (ms1 < ms2).astype(int) * -1
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

} else {

  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }

    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);

  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {

    U32 src2_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));

[#udb:doc:inst:mcolunzip_ew]
=== `mcolunzip.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise column unzip (de-interleave)

Mnemonic::
`mcolunzip.ew md, ms1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x80,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
De-interleaves each row of `ms1` into lower and upper halves in `md`.
+
Let `N = sqrt(AME_NELEM)`. For each row `i` and index `j` in `[0, N/2)`:
+
  `md[i, j]       = ms1[i, 2j]`
  `md[i, j + N/2] = ms1[i, 2j+1]`
+
Even-indexed columns of each row are collected into the lower half of the output;
odd-indexed columns into the upper half.  Inverse of `mcolzip.1d`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
conceptual: de-interleave each row into lower and upper halves
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];

  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::COLUNZIP1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src1_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  U32 N = <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM);
  for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < N; i++) {
    for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < N / 2; j++) {
      U32 e_src_even = i * N pass:[+] 2 * j;
      U32 e_dst_lo = i * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 src_even_regno = e_src_even / src1_elements_per_reg;
      U32 src_even_hi = ((e_src_even pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_even_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 src_even_lo = ((e_src_even pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_even_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_lo_regno = e_dst_lo / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_lo_hi = ((e_dst_lo pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_lo_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_lo_lo = ((e_dst_lo pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_lo_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      M[md pass:[+] dst_lo_regno][dst_lo_hi:dst_lo_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::COLUNZIP1D, src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_even_regno], src1_dtype)[src_even_hi:src_even_lo], src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_even_regno], src1_dtype)[src_even_hi:src_even_lo], dest_dtype), dest_dtype);
      U32 e_src_odd = i * N pass:[+] 2 * j pass:[+] 1;
      U32 e_dst_hi = i * N pass:[+] j pass:[+] N / 2;
      U32 src_odd_regno = e_src_odd / src1_elements_per_reg;
      U32 src_odd_hi = ((e_src_odd pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_odd_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 src_odd_lo = ((e_src_odd pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_odd_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_hi_regno = e_dst_hi / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_hi_hi = ((e_dst_hi pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_hi_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_hi_lo = ((e_dst_hi pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_hi_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      M[md pass:[+] dst_hi_regno][dst_hi_hi:dst_hi_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::COLUNZIP1D, src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_odd_regno], src1_dtype)[src_odd_hi:src_odd_lo], src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_odd_regno], src1_dtype)[src_odd_hi:src_odd_lo], dest_dtype), dest_dtype);
    }
  }
}

<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mcolzip_ew]
=== `mcolzip.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise column zip (interleave)

Mnemonic::
`mcolzip.ew md, ms1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x60,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Interleaves the lower and upper halves of each row of `ms1` into `md`.
+
Let `N = sqrt(AME_NELEM)`. For each row `i` and index `j` in `[0, N/2)`:
+
  `md[i, 2j]   = ms1[i, j]`
  `md[i, 2j+1] = ms1[i, j + N/2]`
+
The lower half of each row occupies even columns in the output; the upper half
occupies odd columns.  Inverse of `mcolunzip.1d`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
conceptual: interleave lower and upper halves of each row
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::COLZIP1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src1_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::COLZIP1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src1_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  U32 N = <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM);
  for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < N; i++) {
    for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < N / 2; j++) {
      U32 e_src_lo = i * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 e_dst_lo = i * N pass:[+] 2 * j;
      U32 src_lo_regno = e_src_lo / src1_elements_per_reg;
      U32 src_lo_hi = ((e_src_lo pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_lo_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 src_lo_lo = ((e_src_lo pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_lo_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_lo_regno = e_dst_lo / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_lo_hi = ((e_dst_lo pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_lo_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_lo_lo = ((e_dst_lo pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_lo_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      M[md pass:[+] dst_lo_regno][dst_lo_hi:dst_lo_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::COLZIP1D, src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_lo_regno], src1_dtype)[src_lo_hi:src_lo_lo], src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_lo_regno], src1_dtype)[src_lo_hi:src_lo_lo], dest_dtype), dest_dtype);
      U32 e_src_hi = i * N pass:[+] j pass:[+] N / 2;
      U32 e_dst_hi = i * N pass:[+] 2 * j pass:[+] 1;
      U32 src_hi_regno = e_src_hi / src1_elements_per_reg;
      U32 src_hi_hi = ((e_src_hi pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_hi_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 src_hi_lo = ((e_src_hi pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_hi_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_hi_regno = e_dst_hi / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_hi_hi = ((e_dst_hi pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_hi_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_hi_lo = ((e_dst_hi pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_hi_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      M[md pass:[+] dst_hi_regno][dst_hi_hi:dst_hi_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::COLZIP1D, src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_hi_regno], src1_dtype)[src_hi_hi:src_hi_lo], src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_hi_regno], src1_dtype)[src_hi_hi:src_hi_lo], dest_dtype), dest_dtype);
    }
  }

<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mconv_ew]
=== `mconv.ew`

Synopsis::
Convert between storage-only and compute datatypes

Mnemonic::
`mconv.ew md, ms1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x5,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Converts element data between a storage-only datatype and a compute datatype.
+
The source datatype is determined from `Md[ms1]` and the destination datatype from `Md[md]`.
Exactly one of the two must be a storage-only datatype (size < `AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE`);
if both or neither are storage-only, `mconv.1d` sets `amestatus.UN` and returns without
modifying any register.
+
**Expand (storage-only → compute):** When `Md[ms1]` is storage-only and `Md[md]` is a
compute datatype, `ms1` holds `pack_factor = AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE / sizeof(Md[ms1])`
packed squares. `mconv.1d` converts each element from the storage datatype to the compute
datatype and writes `pack_factor` result squares to `md`, `md+1`, ..., `md+pack_factor-1`.
The register index `md` must be a multiple of `pack_factor`; otherwise,
`mconv.1d` raises an `Illegal Instruction` exception.
+
**Compress (compute → storage-only):** When `Md[ms1]` is a compute datatype and `Md[md]`
is storage-only, `ms1`, `ms1+1`, ..., `ms1+pack_factor-1` each hold one compute-dtype square.
`mconv.1d` converts each element from the compute datatype to the storage datatype and packs
all `pack_factor` result squares into the single register `md`.
The register index `ms1` must be a multiple of `pack_factor`; otherwise,
`mconv.1d` raises an `Illegal Instruction` exception.
+
The specific element-level conversion (e.g., sign extension, truncation, rounding) is
implementation-defined and discoverable via `amestatus.UN`.



Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms1];
Bits<32> dst_dtype = Md[md];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::CONV1D, dst_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype) == <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dst_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype)) {
    U32 src_element_size_bits = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
    U32 pack_factor = AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE / src_element_size_bits;
    U32 dst_element_size_bits = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dst_dtype);
    if pass:[(]md % pack_factor != 0) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
    if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16 && md pass:[+] pack_factor > 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> packed = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1], src_dtype);
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result = 0;
    for pass:[(]U32 sq = 0; sq < pack_factor; sq++) {
      result = 0;
      for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
        U32 src_lo = (sq * AME_NELEM pass:[+] e) * src_element_size_bits;
        U32 src_hi = src_lo pass:[+] src_element_size_bits - 1;
        Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> element = packed[src_hi:src_lo];
        U32 dst_lo = e * dst_element_size_bits;
        U32 dst_hi = dst_lo pass:[+] dst_element_size_bits - 1;
        result[dst_hi:dst_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::CONV1D, src_dtype, element, src_dtype, element, dst_dtype);
      }
      M[md pass:[+] sq] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dst_dtype);
    }
  } else {
    U32 dst_element_size_bits = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dst_dtype);
    U32 pack_factor = AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE / dst_element_size_bits;
    U32 src_element_size_bits = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
    if pass:[(]ms1 % pack_factor != 0) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
    if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16 && ms1 pass:[+] pack_factor > 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> packed = 0;
    for pass:[(]U32 sq = 0; sq < pack_factor; sq++) {
      Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_data = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] sq], src_dtype);
      for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
        U32 src_lo = e * src_element_size_bits;
        U32 src_hi = src_lo pass:[+] src_element_size_bits - 1;
        Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> element = src_data[src_hi:src_lo];
        U32 dst_lo = (sq * AME_NELEM pass:[+] e) * dst_element_size_bits;
        U32 dst_hi = dst_lo pass:[+] dst_element_size_bits - 1;
        packed[dst_hi:dst_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::CONV1D, src_dtype, element, src_dtype, element, dst_dtype);
      }
    }
    M[md] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]packed, dst_dtype);
  }
}
----

[#udb:doc:inst:mexp2_ew]
=== `mexp2.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise base-2 exponentiation

Mnemonic::
`mexp2.ew md, ms1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x20,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise base-2 exponentiation of the tensor in `ms1`, stored into `md`.
+
For each element, `md[i] = 2^ms1[i]`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = np.exp2(ms1)
----

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::EXP21D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src1_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::EXP21D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src1_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src1_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src1_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src1_regno], src1_dtype);
    U32 src1_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src1_element_value = src1_value[src1_hi_idx:src1_lo_idx];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::EXP21D, src1_dtype, src1_element_value, src1_dtype, src1_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}

[#udb:doc:inst:mgather_ew]
=== `mgather.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise gather (take)

Mnemonic::
`mgather.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x18,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise gather: for each element in each row, uses the corresponding index from `ms2`
to select a column from the same row of `ms1`, and stores the result into `md`.
+
For each row `i` and column `j`:
+
  `md[i,j] = ms1[i, ms2[i,j]]`
+
`ms2` provides integer column indices in the range `[0, sqrt(AME_NELEM))`.
An out-of-range index raises an `Illegal Instruction` exception.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md[i] = ms1[i][ms2[i]]
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
Bits<32> src2_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::GATHER1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src2_nregs == 0) {
    src2_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src2_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src2_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::GATHER1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  U32 N = <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM);
  for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < N; i++) {
    for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < N; j++) {
      U32 e = i * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 idx_regno = e / src2_elements_per_reg;
      U32 idx_hi = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (idx_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 idx_lo = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (idx_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 col_idx = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] idx_regno], src2_dtype)[idx_hi:idx_lo];
      if pass:[(]col_idx >= N) {
        <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
      }
      U32 e_src = i * N pass:[+] col_idx;
      U32 src_regno = e_src / src1_elements_per_reg;
      U32 src_hi = ((e_src pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 src_lo = ((e_src pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_hi = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_lo = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_regno], src1_dtype)[src_hi:src_lo];
      M[md pass:[+] dst_regno][dst_hi:dst_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::GATHER1D, src1_dtype, src_value, src1_dtype, src_value, dest_dtype), dest_dtype);
    }
  }
}
----

[#udb:doc:inst:mhdiff_ew]
=== `mhdiff.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise half-difference

Mnemonic::
`mhdiff.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x3,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise half-difference of the tensors in `ms1` and `ms2`, stored into `md`.
Computes the true half-difference; pairs with `mmean.1d`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = (ms2 - ms1) * 0.5
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];

  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);

    src2_nregs = 1;
  }

  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);

    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }

  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src1_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src1_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src1_regno], src1_dtype);

    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));

[#udb:doc:inst:mhdiff_ew_x]
=== `mhdiff.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar half-difference

Mnemonic::
`mhdiff.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x6,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Computes the elementwise half-difference between a scalar constant from integer register
`xs1` and every element of square `ms2`, stored into `md`.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = (xs1 - ms2[i]) / 2`
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = (xs1 - ms2) / 2
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::HDIFF1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::HDIFF1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar = X[xs1];
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src_regno = e / src_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src_regno], src_dtype);
    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_element_value = scalar[src_element_size - 1:0];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::HDIFF1D, src_dtype, src_element_value, src_dtype, scalar_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}
----

[#udb:doc:inst:mldexp_ew]
=== `mldexp.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise left-shift scale (ldexp)

Mnemonic::
`mldexp.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x12,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise scale of `ms1` by a power of two given by `ms2`, stored into `md`.
+
For each element, `md[i] = ms1[i] * 2^ms2[i]`.
+
Equivalent to C `ldexp` applied elementwise.
Complementary to `mrdexp.1d`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = np.ldexp(ms1, ms2)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src2_nregs == 0) {
    src2_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src2_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src2_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::LDEXP1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src1_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src1_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src1_regno], src1_dtype);
    U32 src1_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_regno = e / src2_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src2_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src2_regno], src2_dtype);
    U32 src2_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src1_element_value = src1_value[src1_hi_idx:src1_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src2_element_value = src2_value[src2_hi_idx:src2_lo_idx];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::LDEXP1D, src1_dtype, src1_element_value, src2_dtype, src2_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}
