<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mldexp_ew_x]
=== `mldexp.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar left-shift scale (ldexp)

Mnemonic::
`mldexp.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x10,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Scales every element of square `ms2` by a power of two given by a scalar integer
from integer register `xs1`, stored into `md`.
+
For each element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = ms2[i] * 2^xs1`
+
The type of the matrix elements is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The scalar exponent is
interpreted as an integer of the maximum supported AME integer datatype (`AME_MAX_INT_DTYPE`).
+
Equivalent to C `ldexp` applied elementwise with a broadcast scalar exponent.
Complementary to `mrdexp.1d`.
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = np.ldexp(ms2, xs1)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms2];
Bits<32> exp_dtype = AME_MAX_INT_DTYPE;
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::LDEXP1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, exp_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  U32 exp_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]exp_dtype);
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::LDEXP1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, exp_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar = X[xs1];
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_exp_element = scalar[exp_element_size - 1:0];
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src_regno = e / src_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src_regno], src_dtype);
    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::LDEXP1D, src_dtype, src_element_value, exp_dtype, scalar_exp_element, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}

[#udb:doc:inst:mldexpacc_ew]
=== `mldexpacc.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise left-shift scale accumulate

Mnemonic::
`mldexpacc.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x13,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise left-shift scale of `ms1` by a power of two given by `ms2`, accumulated into `md`.
+
For each element, `md[i] = md[i] + ms1[i] * 2^ms2[i]`.
+
`md` is both a source and destination: the existing element is read, the scaled value
is added, and the sum is written back.
+
Complementary to `mrdexpacc.1d`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = md + np.ldexp(ms1, ms2)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<32> src2_dtype = Md[ms2];

} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src2_nregs == 0) {
    src2_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src2_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src2_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);

  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::LDEXPACC1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src1_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src1_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src1_regno], src1_dtype);

    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));

    U32 src2_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> dest_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[md pass:[+] dest_regno], dest_dtype);
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src1_element_value = src1_value[src1_hi_idx:src1_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src2_element_value = src2_value[src2_hi_idx:src2_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> dest_current = dest_value[dest_hi_idx:dest_lo_idx];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::LDEXPACC1D, src1_dtype, src1_element_value, src2_dtype, src2_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);

[#udb:doc:inst:mlog2sub_ew]
=== `mlog2sub.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise log2 minus bias

Mnemonic::
`mlog2sub.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x16,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise biased base-2 logarithm: subtracts `ms2` from the base-2 logarithm
of the absolute value of `ms1`, stored into `md`.
+
For each element, `md[i] = log2(|ms1[i]|) - ms2[i]`.
+
Useful for biased-exponent arithmetic, where `ms2` holds the bias value.

[#udb:doc:inst:mlog2sub_ew_x]
=== `mlog2sub.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise log2 minus scalar bias

Mnemonic::
`mlog2sub.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0xe,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Computes the elementwise base-2 logarithm of the absolute value of every element of
square `ms2`, minus a scalar bias from integer register `xs1`, stored into `md`.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar bias value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = log2(|ms2[i]|) - xs1`
+
Useful for biased-exponent arithmetic, where `xs1` holds the bias value.
Complementary to `msublog2.1d.x`.
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = np.log2(np.abs(ms2)) - xs1
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::LOG2SUB1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::LOG2SUB1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar = X[xs1];
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src_regno = e / src_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src_regno], src_dtype);
    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_element_value = scalar[src_element_size - 1:0];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::LOG2SUB1D, src_dtype, src_element_value, src_dtype, scalar_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);

<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mls]
=== `mls`

Synopsis::
Load square from implementation-defined format

Mnemonic::
`mls md, xs1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x40,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Loads a square from memory in the implementation-defined register format into matrix
register `md`.
+
The data in memory must have been previously stored in the implementation-defined
register format (e.g., by a matching `ss` instruction). No datatype conversion is
performed; the in-memory layout is the exact register representation. All elements
are loaded unconditionally. This instruction is correct for both compute and
storage-only dtypes without any special handling.
+
For portable interoperability with other implementations, use
`<%= link_to_udb_doc_inst("mls.rm") %>` or `<%= link_to_udb_doc_inst("mls.cm") %>`.
+
The address must be aligned to the implementation-defined square size or 4KB,
whichever is smaller. Otherwise, `ls` raises a `Load Misaligned` exception.



Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg address = X[xs1];
if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
  if pass:[(]md >= 16) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
}
XReg impl_size_bytes = AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE >> 3;
XReg alignment = <<udb:doc:func:min,min>>pass:[(]impl_size_bytes, 4096);
if pass:[(]address % alignment != 0) {
  <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::LoadAddressMisaligned, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
}
M[md] = <<udb:doc:func:read_memory_ame,read_memory_ame>>pass:[(]address, $encoding, impl_size_bytes);
----


<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mls_cm]
=== `mls.cm`

Synopsis::
Load square from column-major format

Mnemonic::
`mls.cm md, xs1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x20,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Loads a square from memory in column-major format into matrix register `md`.
+
The datatype is determined from `Md[md]`. For compute datatypes
(size >= `AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE`), one square is loaded. For storage-only datatypes
(size < `AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE`), `pack_factor = AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE / sizeof(Md[md])`
squares are loaded and packed into a single M register.
+
The data in memory is stored contiguously in column-major order: within each sub-square,
column `j` immediately follows column `j-1` with no padding. All elements are loaded
unconditionally.
+
The address must be aligned to the total data size
(`pack_factor * AME_NELEM * sizeof(Md[md])`) or 4KB, whichever is smaller.
Otherwise, `ls.cm` raises a `Load Misaligned` exception.



Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg address = X[xs1];
Bits<32> dtype = Md[md];
if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
  if pass:[(]md >= 16) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
}
U32 element_size_bits = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dtype);
U32 element_size_bytes = element_size_bits >> 3;
U32 pack_factor = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dtype) ? (AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE / element_size_bits) : 1;
XReg total_bytes = pack_factor * AME_NELEM * element_size_bytes;
XReg alignment = <<udb:doc:func:min,min>>pass:[(]total_bytes, 4096);
if pass:[(]address % alignment != 0) {
  <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::LoadAddressMisaligned, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
}
Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> tmp = 0;
for pass:[(]U32 sq = 0; sq < pack_factor; sq++) {
  for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM); j++) {
    for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM); i++) {
      U32 element_idx = sq * AME_NELEM pass:[+] j * <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM) pass:[+] i;
      U32 bit_lo = element_idx * element_size_bits;
      U32 bit_hi = bit_lo pass:[+] element_size_bits - 1;
      tmp[bit_hi:bit_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:read_memory_ame,read_memory_ame>>pass:[(]address pass:[+] element_idx * element_size_bytes, $encoding, element_size_bytes);
    }
  }
}
M[md] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_cm_to_impl,ame_xform_cm_to_impl>>pass:[(]tmp, dtype);

<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mls_rm]
=== `mls.rm`

Synopsis::
Load square from row-major format

Mnemonic::
`mls.rm md, xs1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Loads a square from memory in row-major format into matrix register `md`.
+
The datatype is determined from `Md[md]`. For compute datatypes
(size >= `AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE`), one square is loaded. For storage-only datatypes
(size < `AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE`), `pack_factor = AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE / sizeof(Md[md])`
squares are loaded and packed into a single M register.
+
The data in memory is stored contiguously in row-major order: within each sub-square,
row `i` immediately follows row `i-1` with no padding. All elements are loaded
unconditionally.
+
The address must be aligned to the total data size
(`pack_factor * AME_NELEM * sizeof(Md[md])`) or 4KB, whichever is smaller.
Otherwise, `ls.rm` raises a `Load Misaligned` exception.



Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg address = X[xs1];
Bits<32> dtype = Md[md];
if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
  if pass:[(]md >= 16) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
}
U32 element_size_bits = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dtype);
U32 element_size_bytes = element_size_bits >> 3;
U32 pack_factor = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dtype) ? (AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE / element_size_bits) : 1;
XReg total_bytes = pack_factor * AME_NELEM * element_size_bytes;
XReg alignment = <<udb:doc:func:min,min>>pass:[(]total_bytes, 4096);
if pass:[(]address % alignment != 0) {
  <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::LoadAddressMisaligned, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
}
Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> tmp = 0;
for pass:[(]U32 sq = 0; sq < pack_factor; sq++) {
  for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM); i++) {
    for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM); j++) {
      U32 element_idx = sq * AME_NELEM pass:[+] i * <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM) pass:[+] j;
      U32 bit_lo = element_idx * element_size_bits;
      U32 bit_hi = bit_lo pass:[+] element_size_bits - 1;
      tmp[bit_hi:bit_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:read_memory_ame,read_memory_ame>>pass:[(]address pass:[+] element_idx * element_size_bytes, $encoding, element_size_bytes);
    }
  }
}
M[md] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]tmp, dtype);
----

[#udb:doc:inst:mmax_ew]
=== `mmax.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise maximum

Mnemonic::
`mmax.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x5,"type":2}]}

Description::

Used for ReLU, pooling, and clipping.

Bits<32> src2_dtype = Md[ms2];

  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;

    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);

  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;

    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_regno = e / src2_elements_per_reg;

[#udb:doc:inst:mmax_ew_x]
=== `mmax.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar maximum

Mnemonic::
`mmax.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x3,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Computes the elementwise maximum of a scalar constant from integer register `xs1` and
every element of square `ms2`, stored into `md`.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = max(xs1, ms2[i])`
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = np.maximum(xs1, ms2)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MAX1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MAX1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar = X[xs1];
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src_regno = e / src_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src_regno], src_dtype);
    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_element_value = scalar[src_element_size - 1:0];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MAX1D, src_dtype, scalar_element_value, src_dtype, src_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}

+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = (xs1 + ms2[i]) / 2`
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----

----

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]

Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----

=== `mmin.ew`

[#udb:doc:inst:mmin_ew_x]
=== `mmin.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar minimum

Mnemonic::
`mmin.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x2,"type":2}]}
....

Description::

every element of square `ms2`, stored into `md`.

[#udb:doc:inst:mmov_a_m]
=== `mmov.a.m`

Synopsis::
Elementwise unconditional move from accumulator to M register

Mnemonic::
`mmov.a.m md, acc`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":8,"name": 0x4,"type":2},{"bits":2,"name": "acc","type":4},{"bits":10,"name": 0x18,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Copies all `AME_NELEM` elements from accumulator `acc` to the M register
group `md`.
+
The element datatype of `acc` (from `Ad[acc]`) and `md` (from `Md[md]`)
must match; if they differ, `amestatus.UN` is set and `md` is left unchanged.
+
The destination `md` must satisfy the alignment constraint for its datatype:
`md` must be a multiple of the number of M registers consumed by one element.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md[:] = acc.flatten()
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<2> acc = $encoding[21:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src_dtype = Ad[acc];
if pass:[(]dest_dtype[7:0] != src_dtype[7:0]) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  U32 element_size_bits = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  if pass:[(]element_size_bits == 0) {
    CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
  } else {
    U32 dest_nregs = element_size_bits / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
    if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
      dest_nregs = 1;
    }
    U32 elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
    if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
    for pass:[(]U32 dest_regno = 0; dest_regno < dest_nregs; dest_regno++) {
      Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result = 0;
      for pass:[(]U32 local_e = 0; local_e < elements_per_reg; local_e++) {
        U32 e = dest_regno * elements_per_reg pass:[+] local_e;
        U32 acc_bit_lo = e * element_size_bits;
        U32 acc_bit_hi = acc_bit_lo pass:[+] element_size_bits - 1;
        U32 reg_bit_lo = local_e * element_size_bits;
        U32 reg_bit_hi = reg_bit_lo pass:[+] element_size_bits - 1;
        result[reg_bit_hi:reg_bit_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]Acc[acc], src_dtype)[acc_bit_hi:acc_bit_lo];
      }
      M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
    }
  }
}
----


<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mmov_m_m]
=== `mmov.m.m`

Synopsis::
Elementwise unconditional move between M registers

Mnemonic::
`mmov.m.m md, ms`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":8,"name": 0x4,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x2,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Copies all elements from `ms` to `md`.
+
The element datatype of `ms` and `md` must match; if they differ,
`amestatus.UN` is set and `md` is left unchanged.
+
`ms` and `md` must satisfy the same alignment constraints as any other
instruction using that datatype.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = ms.copy()
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms];
if pass:[(]dest_dtype[7:0] != src_dtype[7:0]) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  U32 element_size_bits = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  if pass:[(]element_size_bits == 0) {
    CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
  } else {
    U32 nregs = element_size_bits / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
    if pass:[(]nregs == 0) {
      nregs = 1;
    }
    if pass:[(](ms % nregs) != 0) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
    if pass:[(](md % nregs) != 0) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
    for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < nregs; i++) {
      M[md pass:[+] i] = M[ms pass:[+] i];
    }
  }
}
----

[#udb:doc:inst:mmul_2d]
=== `mmul.2d`

Synopsis::
Matrix multiply

Mnemonic::
`mmul.2d acc, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":8,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":2,"name": "acc","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": 0x8,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Computes the matrix product of `ms1` and `ms2` and stores the result into `acc`,
discarding any previous value in `acc`.
+
`acc[i,k] = sum over j of (ms1[i,j] * ms2[j,k])`
+
For the accumulating form, see `mmacc.2d`.

[source,python]
----
acc = ms1 @ ms2
----

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]

Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]

  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }

    src2_nregs = 1;
  }

    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);

        U32 a_regno = e_a / src1_elements_per_reg;

        U32 b_hi = ((e_b pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (b_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);

      }

      U32 d_lo = ((e_d pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size);

    }
  }
}

[#udb:doc:inst:mmul_ew_x]
=== `mmul.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar multiplication

Mnemonic::
`mmul.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x12,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Multiplies every element of square `ms2` by a scalar constant from integer register
`xs1`, stored into `md`.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = xs1 × ms2[i]`
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = xs1 * ms2
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms2];

} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MUL1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar = X[xs1];
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src_regno = e / src_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src_regno], src_dtype);
    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_element_value = scalar[src_element_size - 1:0];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MUL1D, src_dtype, scalar_element_value, src_dtype, src_element_value, dest_dtype);

[#udb:doc:inst:mmulacc_2d]
=== `mmulacc.2d`

Synopsis::
Matrix multiply accumulate

Mnemonic::
`mmulacc.2d acc, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":8,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":2,"name": "acc","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": 0x8,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x1,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Accumulates the matrix product of `ms1` and `ms2` into `acc`.
+
`acc[i,k] += sum over j of (ms1[i,j] * ms2[j,k])`
+
`acc` is both a source and destination: its current value is read, the matrix
product is added, and the result is written back.
+
For the non-accumulating form, see `mm.2d`.
For the subtracting form, see `mmaccneg.2d`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
acc += ms1 @ ms2
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<2> acc = $encoding[9:8];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
Bits<32> src2_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MMACC1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src2_nregs == 0) {
    src2_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src2_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src2_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MMACC1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  U32 N = <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM);
  for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < N; i++) {
    for pass:[(]U32 k = 0; k < N; k++) {
      U32 e_d = i * N pass:[+] k;
      U32 d_hi = ((e_d pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size);
      U32 d_lo = ((e_d pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size);
      Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> sum = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]Acc[acc], dest_dtype)[d_hi:d_lo];
      for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < N; j++) {
        U32 e_a = i * N pass:[+] j;
        U32 a_regno = e_a / src1_elements_per_reg;
        U32 a_hi = ((e_a pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (a_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
        U32 a_lo = ((e_a pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (a_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
        U32 e_b = j * N pass:[+] k;
        U32 b_regno = e_b / src2_elements_per_reg;
        U32 b_hi = ((e_b pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (b_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
        U32 b_lo = ((e_b pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (b_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
        sum = sum pass:[+] <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MMACC1D, src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] a_regno], src1_dtype)[a_hi:a_lo], src2_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] b_regno], src2_dtype)[b_hi:b_lo], dest_dtype);
      }
      Acc[acc][d_hi:d_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]sum, dest_dtype);
    }
  }
}

[#udb:doc:inst:mmulacc_ew]
=== `mmulacc.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise multiply-accumulate

Mnemonic::
`mmulacc.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x1d,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise multiply-accumulate: multiplies `ms1` by `ms2` elementwise and accumulates
into `md`.
+
`md` is both a source and destination: the existing element is read, the product
`ms1[i] × ms2[i]` is added, and the sum is written back.
+
For each element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = md[i] + ms1[i] × ms2[i]`


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = md + ms1 * ms2
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----

[#udb:doc:inst:mmulacc_ew_x]
=== `mmulacc.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar multiply-accumulate

Mnemonic::
`mmulacc.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x13,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Multiplies every element of square `ms2` by a scalar constant from integer register
`xs1` and accumulates the product into `md`.
+
`md` is both a source and destination: the existing element is read, the scaled value
`xs1 × ms2[i]` is added, and the sum is written back.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = md[i] + xs1 × ms2[i]`
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = md + xs1 * ms2
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MULACC1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar = X[xs1];
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src_regno = e / src_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src_regno], src_dtype);
    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;

[#udb:doc:inst:mmulaccneg_2d]
=== `mmulaccneg.2d`

Synopsis::
Negated matrix multiply accumulate

Mnemonic::
`mmulaccneg.2d acc, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":8,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":2,"name": "acc","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": 0x8,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x3,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Subtracts the matrix product of `ms1` and `ms2` from `acc`.
+
`acc[i,k] -= sum over j of (ms1[i,j] * ms2[j,k])`
+
`acc` is both a source and destination: its current value is read, the matrix
product is subtracted, and the result is written back.
+
For the adding accumulate form, see `mmacc.2d`.

[source,python]
----
acc -= ms1 @ ms2
----

[#udb:doc:inst:mmulaccneg_ew]
=== `mmulaccneg.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise negative multiply-accumulate

Mnemonic::
`mmulaccneg.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x20,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise negative multiply-accumulate: multiplies `ms1` by `ms2` elementwise,
subtracts the product from `md`, and stores the result back into `md`.
+
`md` is both a source and destination: the existing element is read, the product
`ms1[i] × ms2[i]` is subtracted, and the result is written back.
+
For each element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = md[i] - ms1[i] × ms2[i]`


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = md - ms1 * ms2
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
Bits<32> src2_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MULNACC1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;

  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }

  U32 dest_regno = 0;

    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));

    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));

<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mmulaccneg_ew_x]
=== `mmulaccneg.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar negative multiply-accumulate

Mnemonic::
`mmulaccneg.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x16,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Multiplies every element of square `ms2` by a scalar constant from integer register
`xs1`, subtracts the product from `md`, and stores the result back into `md`.
+
`md` is both a source and destination: the existing element is read, the product
`xs1 × ms2[i]` is subtracted, and the result is written back.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = md[i] - xs1 × ms2[i]`
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = md - xs1 * ms2
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MULNACC1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MULNACC1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar = X[xs1];
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src_regno = e / src_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src_regno], src_dtype);
    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> dest_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[md pass:[+] dest_regno], dest_dtype);
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_element_value = scalar[src_element_size - 1:0];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> dest_current = dest_value[dest_hi_idx:dest_lo_idx];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MULNACC1D, src_dtype, scalar_element_value, src_dtype, src_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}

[#udb:doc:inst:mmuladd_ew]
=== `mmuladd.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise fused multiply-add

Mnemonic::
`mmuladd.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x1e,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise fused multiply-add where `md` serves as both the multiplicand and the
destination.
+
`md` is both a source and destination: each existing element is multiplied by the
corresponding element of `ms2`, `ms1` is added, and the result is written back.
+
For each element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = ms1[i] + ms2[i] × md[i]`

[source,python]

----

    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src_regno], src_dtype);
    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> dest_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[md pass:[+] dest_regno], dest_dtype);
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_element_value = scalar[src_element_size - 1:0];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> dest_current = dest_value[dest_hi_idx:dest_lo_idx];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MULADD1D, src_dtype, scalar_element_value, src_dtype, src_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}

[#udb:doc:inst:mmulat_2d]
=== `mmulat.2d`

Synopsis::
Matrix multiply with transposed A

Mnemonic::
`mmulat.2d acc, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":8,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":2,"name": "acc","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": 0x8,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x4,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Computes the matrix product of the transpose of `ms1` with `ms2` and stores the
result into `acc`, discarding any previous value in `acc`.
+
`acc[i,k] = sum over j of (ms1[j,i] * ms2[j,k])`
+
For the accumulating form, see `mmatacc.2d`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
acc = ms1.T @ ms2
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<32> src2_dtype = Md[ms2];

} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src2_nregs == 0) {
    src2_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src2_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src2_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MMAT1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  U32 N = <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM);
  for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < N; i++) {
    for pass:[(]U32 k = 0; k < N; k++) {
      Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> sum = 0;
      for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < N; j++) {
        U32 e_a = j * N pass:[+] i;
        U32 a_regno = e_a / src1_elements_per_reg;
        U32 a_hi = ((e_a pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (a_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
        U32 a_lo = ((e_a pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (a_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
        U32 e_b = j * N pass:[+] k;
        U32 b_regno = e_b / src2_elements_per_reg;
        U32 b_hi = ((e_b pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (b_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
        U32 b_lo = ((e_b pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (b_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
        sum = sum pass:[+] <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MMAT1D, src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] a_regno], src1_dtype)[a_hi:a_lo], src2_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] b_regno], src2_dtype)[b_hi:b_lo], dest_dtype);
      }
      U32 e_d = i * N pass:[+] k;
      U32 d_hi = ((e_d pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size);
      U32 d_lo = ((e_d pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size);
      Acc[acc][d_hi:d_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]sum, dest_dtype);
    }
  }

=== `mmulatacc.2d`

Synopsis::
Matrix multiply with transposed A, accumulate

Mnemonic::
`mmulatacc.2d acc, ms1, ms2`

+

+

  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MMBTACC1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }

    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }

      U32 d_lo = ((e_d pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size);

        U32 a_hi = ((e_a pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (a_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
        U32 a_lo = ((e_a pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (a_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);

[#udb:doc:inst:mmulneg_2d]
=== `mmulneg.2d`

Synopsis::
Negated matrix multiply

Mnemonic::
`mmulneg.2d acc, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":8,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":2,"name": "acc","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": 0x8,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x2,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Computes the negated matrix product of `ms1` and `ms2` and stores the result into `acc`,
discarding any previous value in `acc`.
+
`acc[i,k] = -(sum over j of (ms1[i,j] * ms2[j,k]))`
+
For the accumulating negated form, see `mmaccneg.2d`.

[source,python]

----

    }

    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);

=== `mmulneg.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise negate-multiply

+

[#udb:doc:inst:mmulneg_ew_x]
=== `mmulneg.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar negate-multiply

Mnemonic::
`mmulneg.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x17,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Negates the product of a scalar constant from integer register `xs1` and every element
of square `ms2`, stored into `md`.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = -(xs1 × ms2[i])`
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = -(xs1 * ms2)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::NMUL1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::NMUL1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar = X[xs1];
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src_regno = e / src_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src_regno], src_dtype);
    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_element_value = scalar[src_element_size - 1:0];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::NMUL1D, src_dtype, scalar_element_value, src_dtype, src_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}

[#udb:doc:inst:mmulsub_ew]
=== `mmulsub.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise fused multiply-subtract

Mnemonic::
`mmulsub.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x1f,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise fused multiply-subtract where `md` serves as both the multiplicand and the
destination.
+
`md` is both a source and destination: each existing element is multiplied by the
corresponding element of `ms2`, `ms1` is subtracted from that product, and the result
is written back. Note: this computes `ms1 - ms2 × md`, not `ms2 × md - ms1`.
+
For each element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = ms1[i] - ms2[i] × md[i]`


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = ms1 - ms2 * md
----

[#udb:doc:inst:mmulsub_ew_x]
=== `mmulsub.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar fused multiply-subtract

Mnemonic::
`mmulsub.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x15,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise scalar fused multiply-subtract where `md` serves as both the multiplicand
and the destination.
+
`md` is both a source and destination: each existing element is multiplied by the
corresponding element of `ms2`, that product is subtracted from the scalar `xs1`,
and the result is written back.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = xs1 - ms2[i] × md[i]`
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = xs1 - ms2 * md
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms2];

} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::MULSUB1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }

  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {

    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> dest_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[md pass:[+] dest_regno], dest_dtype);

=== `mor.ew.x`

`mor.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_element_value = scalar[src_element_size - 1:0];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::OR1D, src_dtype, scalar_element_value, src_dtype, src_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}

[#udb:doc:inst:mornot_ew]
=== `mornot.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise bitwise OR-NOT

Mnemonic::
`mornot.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0xa,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise bitwise OR of `ms1` with the bitwise complement of `ms2`, stored into `md`.
+
Useful for setting bits: any bit clear in `ms2` will be set in the result.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = ms1 | ~ms2
----

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]

    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);

    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));

[#udb:doc:inst:mornot_ew_x]
=== `mornot.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar bitwise OR-NOT

Mnemonic::
`mornot.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0xa,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Computes the elementwise bitwise OR of a scalar constant from integer register `xs1`
with the bitwise complement of every element of square `ms2`, stored into `md`.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = xs1 | ~ms2[i]`
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = xs1 | ~ms2
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
