Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ORNOT1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ORNOT1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar = X[xs1];
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src_regno = e / src_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src_regno], src_dtype);
    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_element_value = scalar[src_element_size - 1:0];

[#udb:doc:inst:mprefixadd_col]
=== `mprefixadd.col`

Synopsis::
Elementwise column prefix-sum (inclusive scan)

Mnemonic::
`mprefixadd.col md, ms1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x180,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Computes an inclusive prefix sum (running sum) along each column of `ms1`, stored into `md`.
+
For each row `i` and column `j`:
+
  `md[i,j] = sum over k <= i of ms1[k,j]`
+
`md[0,j] = ms1[0,j]`, `md[1,j] = ms1[0,j] + ms1[1,j]`, and so on.
For the row prefix-sum form, see `mprefixadd.row`.
For the column max-scan form, see `mprefixmax.col`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md[:,j] = np.cumsum(ms1[:,j])
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::PREFIXADDCOL1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src1_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::PREFIXADDCOL1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src1_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  U32 N = <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM);
  for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < N; j++) {
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> running = 0;
    for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < N; i++) {
      U32 e = i * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 src_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
      U32 src_hi = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 src_lo = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      running = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::PREFIXADDCOL1D, src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_regno], src1_dtype)[src_hi:src_lo], dest_dtype, running, dest_dtype);
      U32 dst_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_hi = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_lo = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      M[md pass:[+] dst_regno][dst_hi:dst_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]running, dest_dtype);
    }
  }
}

[#udb:doc:inst:mprefixadd_row]
=== `mprefixadd.row`

Synopsis::
Elementwise row prefix-sum (inclusive scan)

Mnemonic::
`mprefixadd.row md, ms1`

[IMPORTANT]

      U32 e = i * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 src_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
      U32 src_hi = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 src_lo = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      running = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::PREFIXADD1D, src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_regno], src1_dtype)[src_hi:src_lo], dest_dtype, running, dest_dtype);
      U32 dst_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_hi = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_lo = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      M[md pass:[+] dst_regno][dst_hi:dst_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]running, dest_dtype);
    }
  }
}

[#udb:doc:inst:mprefixmax_col]
=== `mprefixmax.col`

Synopsis::
Elementwise column prefix-max (running maximum scan)

Mnemonic::
`mprefixmax.col md, ms1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x1a0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Computes a running maximum (inclusive prefix max) along each column of `ms1`, stored into `md`.
+
For each row `i` and column `j`:
+
  `md[i,j] = max over k <= i of ms1[k,j]`
+
`md[0,j] = ms1[0,j]`, `md[1,j] = max(ms1[0,j], ms1[1,j])`, and so on.
For the row prefix-max form, see `mprefixmax.row`.
For the column add-scan form, see `mprefixadd.col`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md[:,j] = np.maximum.accumulate(ms1[:,j])
----

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]

Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
----

[#udb:doc:inst:mrdexp_ew]
=== `mrdexp.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise right-shift scale

Mnemonic::
`mrdexp.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x14,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise scale of `ms1` by a negative power of two given by `ms2`, stored into `md`.
+
For each element, `md[i] = ms1[i] * 2^(-ms2[i])`.
+
Equivalent to `np.ldexp(ms1, -ms2)`.
Complementary to `mldexp.1d`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = np.ldexp(ms1, -ms2)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];

    src1_nregs = 1;

    src2_nregs = 1;

    dest_nregs = 1;

  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::RDEXP1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);

  U32 dest_regno = 0;

    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src1_element_value = src1_value[src1_hi_idx:src1_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src2_element_value = src2_value[src2_hi_idx:src2_lo_idx];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::RDEXP1D, src1_dtype, src1_element_value, src2_dtype, src2_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);

[#udb:doc:inst:mrdexpacc_ew]
=== `mrdexpacc.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise right-shift scale accumulate

Mnemonic::
`mrdexpacc.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x15,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise right-shift scale of `ms1` by a negative power of two given by `ms2`,
accumulated into `md`.
+
For each element, `md[i] = md[i] + ms1[i] * 2^(-ms2[i])`.
+
`md` is both a source and destination: the existing element is read, the scaled value
is added, and the sum is written back.
+
Complementary to `mldexpacc.1d`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = md + np.ldexp(ms1, -ms2)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<32> src2_dtype = Md[ms2];

} else {

  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }

  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src2_nregs == 0) {
    src2_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src2_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src2_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);

  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::RDEXPACC1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src1_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src1_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src1_regno], src1_dtype);
    U32 src1_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_regno = e / src2_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src2_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src2_regno], src2_dtype);
    U32 src2_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> dest_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[md pass:[+] dest_regno], dest_dtype);
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src1_element_value = src1_value[src1_hi_idx:src1_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src2_element_value = src2_value[src2_hi_idx:src2_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> dest_current = dest_value[dest_hi_idx:dest_lo_idx];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::RDEXPACC1D, src1_dtype, src1_element_value, src2_dtype, src2_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}

[#udb:doc:inst:mreduceadd_col]
=== `mreduceadd.col`

Synopsis::
Elementwise column reduce (add)

Mnemonic::
`mreduceadd.col md, ms1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x140,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Reduces each column of `ms1` by addition and broadcasts the result to all rows of the
corresponding column in `md`.
+
For each row `i` and column `j`:
+
  `md[i,j] = sum over k of ms1[k,j]`
+
All rows in each output column receive the same value (the column sum).
For the row-reduction form, see `mreduceadd.row`.
For the column max-reduction form, see `mreducemax.col`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md[:,j] = np.sum(ms1[:,j])
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::REDUCEADDCOL1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src1_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::REDUCEADDCOL1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src1_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  U32 N = <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM);
  for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < N; j++) {
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> col_result = 0;
    for pass:[(]U32 k = 0; k < N; k++) {
      U32 e_src = k * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 src_regno = e_src / src1_elements_per_reg;
      U32 src_hi = ((e_src pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 src_lo = ((e_src pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      col_result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::REDUCEADDCOL1D, src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_regno], src1_dtype)[src_hi:src_lo], dest_dtype, col_result, dest_dtype);
    }
    for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < N; i++) {
      U32 e_dst = i * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 dst_regno = e_dst / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_hi = ((e_dst pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_lo = ((e_dst pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);

    }
  }

  U32 N = <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM);
  for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < N; i++) {
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> row_result = 0;
    for pass:[(]U32 k = 0; k < N; k++) {
      U32 e_src = i * N pass:[+] k;
      U32 src_regno = e_src / src1_elements_per_reg;
      U32 src_hi = ((e_src pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 src_lo = ((e_src pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      row_result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::REDUCEMAX1D, src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_regno], src1_dtype)[src_hi:src_lo], dest_dtype, row_result, dest_dtype);
    }
    for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < N; j++) {
      U32 e_dst = i * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 dst_regno = e_dst / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_hi = ((e_dst pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_lo = ((e_dst pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      M[md pass:[+] dst_regno][dst_hi:dst_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]row_result, dest_dtype);
    }
  }
}

<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mrowunzip_ew]
=== `mrowunzip.ew`

Synopsis::
Row unzip (de-interleave rows)

Mnemonic::
`mrowunzip.ew md, ms1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0xa0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
De-interleaves the rows of `ms1` into the destination register pair (`md`, `md+1`).
+
Let `N = sqrt(AME_NELEM)`. For each row `k` in `[0, N)` and column `j`:
+
  `md[k,   j] = ms1[2k,   j]`   (even rows of the source)
  `md+1[k, j] = ms1[2k+1, j]`   (odd rows of the source)
+
The even-indexed rows of `ms1` are collected into `md`; the odd-indexed rows
into `md+1`.  `ms1` is treated as a conceptual `2N`-row matrix stored across
(`ms1`, `ms1+1`): rows `0..N-1` from `ms1`, rows `N..2N-1` from `ms1+1`.
+
`md` must be even-aligned.  Inverse of `mrowzip.1d`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
conceptual: de-interleave rows into two output registers
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];

  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ROWUNZIP1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src1_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % 2) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  U32 N = <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM);
  for pass:[(]U32 k = 0; k < N; k++) {
    for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < N; j++) {
      U32 e_dst = k * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 src_row_even = 2 * k;
      U32 src_reg_even = src_row_even / N;
      U32 src_local_even = src_row_even % N;
      U32 e_src_even = src_local_even * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 src_even_regno = e_src_even / src1_elements_per_reg;
      U32 src_even_hi = ((e_src_even pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_even_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 src_even_lo = ((e_src_even pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_even_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_md_regno = e_dst / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_md_hi = ((e_dst pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_md_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_md_lo = ((e_dst pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_md_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      M[md pass:[+] dst_md_regno][dst_md_hi:dst_md_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ROWUNZIP1D, src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_reg_even pass:[+] src_even_regno], src1_dtype)[src_even_hi:src_even_lo], src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_reg_even pass:[+] src_even_regno], src1_dtype)[src_even_hi:src_even_lo], dest_dtype), dest_dtype);
      U32 src_row_odd = 2 * k pass:[+] 1;
      U32 src_reg_odd = src_row_odd / N;
      U32 src_local_odd = src_row_odd % N;
      U32 e_src_odd = src_local_odd * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 src_odd_regno = e_src_odd / src1_elements_per_reg;
      U32 src_odd_hi = ((e_src_odd pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_odd_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 src_odd_lo = ((e_src_odd pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_odd_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_md1_regno = e_dst / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_md1_hi = ((e_dst pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_md1_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_md1_lo = ((e_dst pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_md1_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      M[(md pass:[+] 1) pass:[+] dst_md1_regno][dst_md1_hi:dst_md1_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ROWUNZIP1D, src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_reg_odd pass:[+] src_odd_regno], src1_dtype)[src_odd_hi:src_odd_lo], src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_reg_odd pass:[+] src_odd_regno], src1_dtype)[src_odd_hi:src_odd_lo], dest_dtype), dest_dtype);
    }

[#udb:doc:inst:mrowzip_ew]
=== `mrowzip.ew`

Synopsis::
Row zip (interleave rows from two inputs)

Mnemonic::
`mrowzip.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x1b,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Interleaves rows from two input registers `ms1` and `ms2` into the destination
register pair (`md`, `md+1`).
+
Let `N = sqrt(AME_NELEM)`. For each row `i` in `[0, N)` and column `j`:
+
  `md[i, j]     = ms1[i/2, j]`   when `i` is even  (i.e. `md[2k,   j] = ms1[k, j]`)
  `md[i, j]     = ms2[i/2, j]`   when `i` is odd   (i.e. `md[2k+1, j] = ms2[k, j]`)
+
`md` must be even-aligned.  Rows from `ms1` (A0) appear at even positions and rows
from `ms2` (A1) appear at odd positions within the register pair.
+
The destination register pair spans `2N` logical rows across (`md`, `md+1`):
rows `0..N-1` are in `md`, rows `N..2N-1` are in `md+1`.
+
Inverse of `mrowunzip.1d`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
conceptual: interleave rows from two inputs
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ROWZIP1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % 2) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {

  }
  U32 N = <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM);

      M[md pass:[+] out_reg_even pass:[+] dst_even_regno][dst_even_hi:dst_even_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::ROWZIP1D, src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src1_regno], src1_dtype)[src1_hi:src1_lo], src1_dtype, <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src1_regno], src1_dtype)[src1_hi:src1_lo], dest_dtype), dest_dtype);

<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mscatadd_col]
=== `mscatadd.col`

Synopsis::
Elementwise column scatter-add

Mnemonic::
`mscatadd.col md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x22,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise column scatter-add: routes each element of `ms1` to a destination row
in `md` determined by the corresponding index in `ms2`, and accumulates with addition.
+
For each row `i` and column `j`:
+
  `md[ms2[i,j], j] += ms1[i,j]`
+
`md` is both a source and destination: elements at the target rows are read,
the contribution from `ms1` is added, and the result is written back.
+
`ms2` provides integer row indices in the range `[0, sqrt(AME_NELEM))`.
Multiple elements may scatter to the same destination row; all contributions are accumulated.
An out-of-range index raises an `Illegal Instruction` exception.
+
For the row scatter-add form, see `mscatadd.row`.
For the column scatter-max form, see `mscatmax.col`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
np.add.at(md[:,j], ms2[:,j], ms1[:,j])
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
Bits<32> src2_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SCATADDCOL1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src2_nregs == 0) {
    src2_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src2_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src2_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SCATADDCOL1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  U32 N = <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM);
  for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < N; i++) {
    for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < N; j++) {
      U32 e = i * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 idx_regno = e / src2_elements_per_reg;
      U32 idx_hi = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (idx_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 idx_lo = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (idx_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 row_idx = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] idx_regno], src2_dtype)[idx_hi:idx_lo];
      if pass:[(]row_idx >= N) {
        <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
      }
      U32 src_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
      U32 src_hi = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 src_lo = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 e_dst = row_idx * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 dst_regno = e_dst / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_hi = ((e_dst pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_lo = ((e_dst pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_regno], src1_dtype)[src_hi:src_lo];
      Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> dst_current = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[md pass:[+] dst_regno], dest_dtype)[dst_hi:dst_lo];
      M[md pass:[+] dst_regno][dst_hi:dst_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SCATADDCOL1D, src1_dtype, src_value, dest_dtype, dst_current, dest_dtype), dest_dtype);
    }
  }
}

[#udb:doc:inst:mscatadd_row]
=== `mscatadd.row`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scatter-add

Mnemonic::
`mscatadd.row md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x19,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise scatter-add: routes each element of `ms1` to a destination column
in `md` determined by the corresponding index in `ms2`, and accumulates with addition.
+
For each row `i` and column `j`:
+
  `md[i, ms2[i,j]] += ms1[i,j]`
+
`md` is both a source and destination: elements at the target columns are read,
the contribution from `ms1` is added, and the result is written back.
+
`ms2` provides integer column indices in the range `[0, sqrt(AME_NELEM))`.
Multiple elements may scatter to the same destination column; all contributions are accumulated.
An out-of-range index raises an `Illegal Instruction` exception.
+
For the row scatter-max form, see `mscatmax.row`.
For the column scatter-add form, see `mscatadd.col`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
np.add.at(md[i], ms2[i], ms1[i])
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
Bits<32> src2_dtype = Md[ms2];

  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);

    src1_nregs = 1;
  }

  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src2_nregs == 0) {
    src2_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src2_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src2_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SCATADD1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {

    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {

[#udb:doc:inst:mscatmax_col]
=== `mscatmax.col`

Synopsis::
Elementwise column scatter-max

Mnemonic::
`mscatmax.col md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x23,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise column scatter-max: routes each element of `ms1` to a destination row
in `md` determined by the corresponding index in `ms2`, and accumulates with maximum.
+
For each row `i` and column `j`:
+
  `md[ms2[i,j], j] = max(md[ms2[i,j], j], ms1[i,j])`
+
`md` is both a source and destination: elements at the target rows are read,
the maximum with the incoming value is taken, and the result is written back.
+
`ms2` provides integer row indices in the range `[0, sqrt(AME_NELEM))`.
Multiple elements may scatter to the same destination row; all contributions are reduced.
An out-of-range index raises an `Illegal Instruction` exception.
+
For the row scatter-max form, see `mscatmax.row`.
For the column scatter-add form, see `mscatadd.col`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
np.maximum.at(md[:,j], ms2[:,j], ms1[:,j])
----

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]

Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----

  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  U32 N = <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM);
  for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < N; i++) {
    for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < N; j++) {
      U32 e = i * N pass:[+] j;
      U32 idx_regno = e / src2_elements_per_reg;
      U32 idx_hi = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (idx_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 idx_lo = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (idx_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 col_idx = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] idx_regno], src2_dtype)[idx_hi:idx_lo];
      if pass:[(]col_idx >= N) {
        <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
      }
      U32 src_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
      U32 src_hi = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 src_lo = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 e_dst = i * N pass:[+] col_idx;
      U32 dst_regno = e_dst / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_hi = ((e_dst pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_lo = ((e_dst pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_regno], src1_dtype)[src_hi:src_lo];
      Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> dst_current = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[md pass:[+] dst_regno], dest_dtype)[dst_hi:dst_lo];
      M[md pass:[+] dst_regno][dst_hi:dst_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SCATMAX1D, src1_dtype, src_value, dest_dtype, dst_current, dest_dtype), dest_dtype);
    }
  }
}
----

[#udb:doc:inst:mselge_ew]
=== `mselge.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise predicated select (non-negative)

Mnemonic::
`mselge.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0xe,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise predicated select using the non-negative sign of `ms1` to gate `ms2` into `md`.
+
For each element, `md[i] = ms2[i]` if `ms1[i] >= 0` (sign bit clear),
otherwise `md[i] = 0`.
+
`ms1` serves as the predicate register: any non-negative value is treated as true.
This allows comparison results or arithmetic sign values to be used directly
as predicates without normalization.
+
Complementary to `mcsellt.1d`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = np.where(ms1 >= 0, ms2, 0)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----

    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);

=== `msellt.ew`

[#udb:doc:inst:msettyp]
=== `msettyp`

Synopsis::

Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];

[#udb:doc:inst:mshift_ew]
=== `mshift.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise row shift by constant offset

Mnemonic::
`mshift.ew md, ms1, imm`

Pseudoinstructions::
`mshift.p1 md, ms1` when `imm == 1`
`mshift.m1 md, ms1` when `imm == -1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x6,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": "imm","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": 0x0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise shift of each row of `ms1` by a signed immediate offset `imm`, stored into `md`.
+
For each row `i` and column `j`:
+
  `md[i,j] = ms1[i, j + imm]`  if `0 <= j + imm < sqrt(AME_NELEM)`, otherwise `md[i,j] = 0`.
+
Elements shifted beyond the row boundary are filled with zero (no wrap-around).
The immediate is a 7-bit signed value, giving a range of −64 to +63.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
conceptual: md[i] = np.roll(ms1[i], -imm) with zero-fill
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<7> imm = $encoding[26:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SHIFT1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src1_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SHIFT1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src1_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  U32 N = <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM);
  Bits<32> shift = $signed+++(+++imm);
  for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < N; i++) {
    for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < N; j++) {
      U32 e_out = i * N pass:[+] j;
      Bits<32> src_j = j pass:[+] shift;
      U32 dst_regno = e_out / dest_elements_per_reg;
      U32 dst_hi = ((e_out pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      U32 dst_lo = ((e_out pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dst_regno * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
      if pass:[(]$signed+++(+++src_j) >= 0 && $signed+++(+++src_j) < N) {
        Bits<32> e_src = i * N pass:[+] src_j;
        Bits<32> src_regno = $signed+++(+++e_src) / src1_elements_per_reg;
        U32 src_hi = ((e_src pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - ($signed+++(+++src_regno) * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
        U32 src_lo = ((e_src pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - ($signed+++(+++src_regno) * AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE);
        Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src_regno], src1_dtype)[src_hi:src_lo];
        M[md pass:[+] dst_regno][dst_hi:dst_lo] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SHIFT1D, src1_dtype, src_value, src1_dtype, src_value, dest_dtype), dest_dtype);
      } else {
        M[md pass:[+] dst_regno][dst_hi:dst_lo] = 0;
      }
    }
  }
}
----

[#udb:doc:inst:mss]
=== `mss`

Synopsis::
Store square to implementation-defined format

Mnemonic::
`mss ms1, xs1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0xa0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Stores a square from matrix register `ms1` into memory in the implementation-defined
register format.
+
The data written to memory is in the same implementation-defined format used by the
matching load instruction (`ls`). No datatype conversion is performed. All elements
are stored unconditionally. This instruction is correct for both compute and
storage-only dtypes without any special handling.
+
For portable interoperability with other implementations, use
`<%= link_to_udb_doc_inst("mss.rm") %>` or `<%= link_to_udb_doc_inst("mss.cm") %>`.
+
The address must be aligned to the implementation-defined square size or 4KB,
whichever is smaller. Otherwise, `ss` raises a `Store/AMO Misaligned` exception.



Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg address = X[xs1];
if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
  if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
}
XReg impl_size_bytes = AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE >> 3;
XReg alignment = <<udb:doc:func:min,min>>pass:[(]impl_size_bytes, 4096);
if pass:[(]address % alignment != 0) {
  <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::StoreAmoAddressMisaligned, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
}
<<udb:doc:func:write_memory_ame,write_memory_ame>>pass:[(]address, $encoding, M[ms1], impl_size_bytes);
----


<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mss_cm]
=== `mss.cm`

Synopsis::
Store square to column-major format

Mnemonic::
`mss.cm ms1, xs1`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x80,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Stores a square from matrix register `ms1` into memory in column-major format.
+
The datatype is determined from `Md[ms1]`. For compute datatypes
(size >= `AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE`), one square is stored. For storage-only datatypes
(size < `AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE`), `pack_factor = AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE / sizeof(Md[ms1])`
squares are unpacked from the single M register and stored.
+
The data is written contiguously in column-major order: within each sub-square,
column `j` immediately follows column `j-1` with no padding. All elements are stored
unconditionally.
+
The address must be aligned to the total data size
(`pack_factor * AME_NELEM * sizeof(Md[ms1])`) or 4KB, whichever is smaller.
Otherwise, `ss.cm` raises a `Store/AMO Misaligned` exception.



Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg address = X[xs1];
Bits<32> dtype = Md[ms1];
if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
  if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
}
U32 element_size_bits = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dtype);
U32 element_size_bytes = element_size_bits >> 3;
U32 pack_factor = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dtype) ? (AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE / element_size_bits) : 1;
XReg total_bytes = pack_factor * AME_NELEM * element_size_bytes;
XReg alignment = <<udb:doc:func:min,min>>pass:[(]total_bytes, 4096);
if pass:[(]address % alignment != 0) {
  <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::StoreAmoAddressMisaligned, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
}
Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> tmp = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_cm,ame_xform_impl_to_cm>>pass:[(]M[ms1], dtype);
for pass:[(]U32 sq = 0; sq < pack_factor; sq++) {
  for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM); j++) {
    for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM); i++) {
      U32 element_idx = sq * AME_NELEM pass:[+] j * <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM) pass:[+] i;
      U32 bit_lo = element_idx * element_size_bits;
      U32 bit_hi = bit_lo pass:[+] element_size_bits - 1;
      <<udb:doc:func:write_memory_ame,write_memory_ame>>pass:[(]address pass:[+] element_idx * element_size_bytes, $encoding, tmp[bit_hi:bit_lo], element_size_bytes);
    }
  }
}
----


<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mss_rm]
=== `mss.rm`

Synopsis::
Store square to row-major format

Mnemonic::
`mss.rm ms1, xs1`

+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]

....

Description::

+

(size >= `AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE`), one square is stored. For storage-only datatypes

for pass:[(]U32 sq = 0; sq < pack_factor; sq++) {
  for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM); i++) {
    for pass:[(]U32 j = 0; j < <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM); j++) {
      U32 element_idx = sq * AME_NELEM pass:[+] i * <<udb:doc:func:sqrt,sqrt>>pass:[(]AME_NELEM) pass:[+] j;
      U32 bit_lo = element_idx * element_size_bits;
      U32 bit_hi = bit_lo pass:[+] element_size_bits - 1;
      <<udb:doc:func:write_memory_ame,write_memory_ame>>pass:[(]address pass:[+] element_idx * element_size_bytes, $encoding, tmp[bit_hi:bit_lo], element_size_bytes);

[#udb:doc:inst:msub_ew]
=== `msub.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise subtraction

Mnemonic::
`msub.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x1,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Vector subtraction of the tensors in `ms1` and `ms2`, stored into `md`.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = ms2 - ms1
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> ms1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src1_dtype = Md[ms1];
Bits<32> src2_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SUB1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src1_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src2_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src1_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src1_dtype);
  U32 src1_nregs = src1_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src1_nregs == 0) {
    src1_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src1_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src1_nregs;
  U32 src2_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src2_dtype);
  U32 src2_nregs = src2_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src2_nregs == 0) {
    src2_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src2_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src2_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SUB1D, dest_dtype, src1_dtype, src2_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms1 >= 16 || ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms1 % src1_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src2_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src1_regno = e / src1_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src1_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms1 pass:[+] src1_regno], src1_dtype);
    U32 src1_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src1_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src1_element_size) - (src1_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_regno = e / src2_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src2_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src2_regno], src2_dtype);
    U32 src2_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src2_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src2_element_size) - (src2_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src1_element_value = src1_value[src1_hi_idx:src1_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src2_element_value = src2_value[src2_hi_idx:src2_lo_idx];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SUB1D, src1_dtype, src1_element_value, src2_dtype, src2_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}

[#udb:doc:inst:msub_ew_x]
=== `msub.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar subtraction

Mnemonic::
`msub.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x1,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Subtracts every element of square `ms2` from a scalar constant from integer register `xs1`,
stored into `md`.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = xs1 - ms2[i]`
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = xs1 - ms2
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<32> dest_dtype = Md[md];
Bits<32> src_dtype = Md[ms2];
if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SUB1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else if pass:[(]<<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]dest_dtype) || <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_is_storage_only,ame_dtype_is_storage_only>>pass:[(]src_dtype)) {
  CSR[<<udb:doc:csr:amestatus,amestatus>>].<<udb:doc:csr_field:amestatus:UN,UN>> = 1;
} else {
  U32 src_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]src_dtype);
  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SUB1D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(]AME_NUM_M_REGS == 16) {
    if pass:[(]ms2 >= 16 || md >= 16) {
      <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
    }
  }
  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar = X[xs1];
  Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> result;
  U32 dest_regno = 0;
  for pass:[(]U32 e = 0; e < AME_NELEM; e++) {
    U32 src_regno = e / src_elements_per_reg;
    Bits<AME_MAX_SQUARE_SIZE> src_value = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_impl_to_rm,ame_xform_impl_to_rm>>pass:[(]M[ms2 pass:[+] src_regno], src_dtype);
    U32 src_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    dest_regno = e / dest_elements_per_reg;
    U32 dest_hi_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    U32 dest_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * dest_element_size) - (dest_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_element_value = scalar[src_element_size - 1:0];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SUB1D, src_dtype, src_element_value, src_dtype, scalar_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}

<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:msublog2_ew]
=== `msublog2.ew`

Synopsis::
Elementwise bias minus log2

Mnemonic::
`msublog2.ew md, ms1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "ms1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x17,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Elementwise complementary biased base-2 logarithm: subtracts the base-2 logarithm
of the absolute value of `ms1` from `ms2`, stored into `md`.
+
For each element, `md[i] = ms2[i] - log2(|ms1[i]|)`.
+
Useful for biased-exponent arithmetic, where `ms2` holds the bias value.
Complementary to `mlog2sub.1d`.


NumPy Equivalent::

[#udb:doc:inst:msublog2_ew_x]
=== `msublog2.ew.x`

Synopsis::
Elementwise scalar bias minus log2

Mnemonic::
`msublog2.ew.x md, xs1, ms2`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "md","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "xs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "ms2","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0xf,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Subtracts the elementwise base-2 logarithm of the absolute value of every element of
square `ms2` from a scalar constant from integer register `xs1`, stored into `md`.
+
The type of the scalar is determined by `Md[ms2]`. The lower `sizeof(Md[ms2])` bits of
`xs1` are used as the scalar bias value for every element position `i`:
+
  `md[i] = xs1 - log2(|ms2[i]|)`
+
Useful for biased-exponent arithmetic, where `xs1` holds the bias value.
Complementary to `mlog2sub.1d.x`.
+
If either `Md[md]` or `Md[ms2]` is uninitialized (zero), or the datatype combination
is not supported, `amestatus.UN` is set and no register is written.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
md = xs1 - np.log2(np.abs(ms2))
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> md = $encoding[11:7];
Bits<5> xs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> ms2 = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]

} else {

  U32 src_nregs = src_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]src_nregs == 0) {
    src_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 src_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / src_nregs;
  U32 dest_element_size = <<udb:doc:func:ame_dtype_val_to_size,ame_dtype_val_to_size>>pass:[(]dest_dtype);
  U32 dest_nregs = dest_element_size / AME_UNIT_DATATYPE_SIZE;
  if pass:[(]dest_nregs == 0) {
    dest_nregs = 1;
  }
  U32 dest_elements_per_reg = AME_NELEM / dest_nregs;
  if pass:[(]!<<udb:doc:func:ame_op_supported,ame_op_supported>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::SUBLOG21D, dest_dtype, src_dtype, src_dtype)) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);

    }

  if pass:[(](ms2 % src_nregs) != 0) {
    <<udb:doc:func:raise,raise>>pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, <<udb:doc:func:mode,mode>>pass:[(]), $encoding);
  }
  if pass:[(](md % dest_nregs) != 0) {

    U32 src_lo_idx = ((e pass:[+] 1) * src_element_size) - (src_regno * (AME_MATRIX_REGISTER_SIZE));

    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> src_element_value = src_value[src_hi_idx:src_lo_idx];
    Bits<AME_MAX_DTYPE_SIZE> scalar_element_value = scalar[src_element_size - 1:0];
    result = <<udb:doc:func:ame_op,ame_op>>pass:[(]AmeOperation::XOR1D, src_dtype, scalar_element_value, src_dtype, src_element_value, dest_dtype);
  }
  M[md pass:[+] dest_regno] = <<udb:doc:func:ame_xform_rm_to_impl,ame_xform_rm_to_impl>>pass:[(]result, dest_dtype);
}
----


<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:mzero_2d]
=== `mzero.2d`

Synopsis::
Clear accumulator tile

Mnemonic::
`mzero.2d acc`

Encoding::
+
[IMPORTANT]
Encodings have not been allocated yet. This is just a placeholder.
+
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":8,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":2,"name": "acc","type":4},{"bits":22,"name": 0x40008,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Writes zero to every element of `acc`.
+
Typically used to initialize an accumulator before a matrix multiply sequence.


NumPy Equivalent::
[source,python]
----
acc = np.zeros_like(acc)
----

Decode Variables::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<2> acc = $encoding[9:8];
----
